< Text>
Seriously one of the most beautiful beaches I've ever seen and I've lived in LA and South Florida.

We went here to shoot the bioluminescence earlier this year. It was perfectly dark (we stayed away from the pier) and the pictures came out beautifully. There were stay at home orders in LA County but not in OC so it was great to take a breather. Parking was really easy because of COVID, everything around the beach was on shorter hours or closed so there was plenty of parking.</Text>

< text>
Clean beach, strong rip tide, life guards on duty. Everything that makes the ocean fun! Just don't let the kids wander too far into the surf bc the waves really sneak up on you sometimes! Paved walking paths take you down to about 25ft before the water too which was very helpful with hands full of coolers, chairs, and umbrellas!<//text>

< text>
I cannot say enough great things about the maintenance staff here! Since moving in October of last year (from out of state), they have been pleasant and courteous with every request. I have two dogs (one is a new and very vocal rescue), so I have begun noting that I need to be home for my work orders.

During this time of COVID, they called to schedule an appointment to fix a sticking gas burner. On the day of the appointment, they knocked, but I asked that they reschedule as I needed to take one of the dogs to an emergency vet appointment. Both guys were very understanding and told me that they could be back later on in the day, to which I agreed. Unfortunately, the vet appointment took longer than anticipated, so I missed the time a second time!

I resubmitted the work order a week later with a note for a Tuesday or Wednesday date. On Monday afternoon, the maintenance techs gave me a call to set a time on Tuesday afternoon. They arrived promptly, and quickly fixed the issue, and then had me test it to make sure that everything was working well. While they were in the apartment, I asked about a few minor things (replacing blinds and the air filter), and they offered to get the replacements for me right then and there.

Anthony (who is the newest maintenance technician) made me feel at ease with his amazing customer service. Instead of silently doing the task in the kitchen while I was in the living room, he introduced himself and was very friendly while being trained by Frank.

Frank was quick and efficient, and did everything with a smile. He explained everything to me that he was doing as he did it, and was the one to offer to check the vents after I asked. He has great insight and was so polite with my thousands of questions.

If you have any concerns about any small issues in the apartments here (it happens everywhere), then you should feel comfortable knowing these guys have got you covered!<//text>

<rating>5<//rating>< text>
The Villas At Towngate is my home and I'm happy I chose here for my first apartment. I love the layout of my apartment and I always get compliments on the pool area and kind staff.
My only complaints are NO pets, so I had to leave my cat at home with my mother; parking can be difficult, and parking can be hard to find sometimes. Keep in mind you get 3 passes for guests. Make sure they place them on their cars or they will be towed. There is also parking on the street and you could park at Winco and walk over to the Villas.
For a single woman stepping out on her own I have to say THANK YOU to the maintenance crew. They are always on top of it to help me. My air condition was acting up and they came early the next day to fix it. On another occasion a guest messed with my alarm system and it went off like crazy and wouldn't turn off. Maintenance and security came to make sure everything was okay and handled the minor emergency quickly. Maintenance are always polite and you can request they call before entering or allow them to enter while you're away. Security walks about sometimes but anytime I called they came quickly to either quiet a loud nuisance, etc. And the front desk is always helpful during their hours to handle minor concerns like neighbor disputes. This is a friendly location for all kinds of people from families to single occupants.
I might pay a bit more than the rest of the MoVal area for my one bedroom but I'm guaranteed safe. I left my door open accidentally one night and nothing bad happened. I've also never seen a vehicle broken into like other apartment complexes.<//text>

PARKING: A bit limited for guests, but residents have reserved spaces if registered. Your car will get towed if you don't follow the rules...duh... This is to respect those who do!

< Text>
The library locates at the heart of Encinitas with a fantastic view of the ocean. It is a great place to hang out to browse magazines, read books, and study. It has plenty of sitting spaces and study rooms. The staffs are friendly and helpful. It also has a coffee stand outside of the library so you can get a drink during your study break. Parking is not an issue since there are ample parking spaces. It also has a bookstore where you can find some used books at good price and its proceeds will benefit the library. All in all, a great public library with good facilities and great view!</Text>

<Time>1485470532262<//Time><Rate>4</Rate><Review>Very comfortable, bright, modern facility and amenities, great views through large wrapping windows and friendly staff. I usually find a cozy seat in the quiet SW corner with an ottoman and peaceful ocean view; pop the earbuds in and get to work. 5 stars only if they had a few partitioned work spaces to keep distractions to a min.

Two important things I didn't see other reivews mention is free access to WIFI and POWER:
1)WIFI is free and has good coverage throughout, but it's open/unsecured like most hotspots are (e.g. coffeshops) and has some built-in restrictions to content access. Ping/Upload/Download speeds are modest but effective.

2) POWER outlets may be hard to find. HINT...look to the floor! They're tucked away in rectangular floor boxes as the library design uses a raised access floor system for HVAC and other utilities (leaves the open ceiling space look much cleaner)...see photos.<//Review>< Pics>

< user_id>
103664024913169452741< /user_id>
<Text>Incredible Park that has seen dramatic improvements over the past few years. To name a few: brand new Olympic sized swimming pool that is kept in excellent condition, 2 brand new full sized basketball courts with smooth paving, updated playground for children.

Other amenities include 2 full tennis courts, soccer fields, baseball diamonds, and a skate park. In my opinion no other neighborhood park in LA County comes close.  There is plenty of room for everyone and the grounds are kept up.

My only recommendation would be to install some water fountains that also include a dog fountain at the bottom since so many people walk their dogs there.

There is also the South side of the park that is below the 60 freeway that can be accessed via foot bridge. It includes a large pond that is stocked with fish to enjoy fishing and a small ampitheatre.

To the gentleman who posted a review regarding no shade on the playground, I disagree, the playground and park itself is surrounded with plenty of trees.<//Text>< resp>
